  <div class="markdown-body">
    <h2>v1.5.1</h2>
<h3>2020-09-16</h3>
<h3>Download</h3>
<p><a href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.5.1">https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.5.1</a></p>
<h3>Container Image</h3>
<p><code>velero/velero:v1.5.1</code></p>
<h3>Documentation</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.5/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.5/</a></p>
<h3>Upgrading</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.5/upgrade-to-1.5/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.5/upgrade-to-1.5/</a></p>
<h3>Highlights</h3>
<ul>
<li>Auto Volume Backup Using Restic with <code>--default-volumes-to-restic</code> flag</li>
<li>DeleteItemAction plugins</li>
<li>Code modernization</li>
<li>Restore Hooks: InitContianer Restore Hooks and Exec Restore Hooks</li>
</ul>
<h3>All Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="running_man" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f3c3-2642.png">🏃‍♂️</g-emoji> add shortnames for CRDs (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="696249390" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2911" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2911/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2911">#2911</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ashish-amarnath/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ashish-amarnath">@ashish-amarnath</a>)</li>

(<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="631155162" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2610" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2610/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2610">#2610</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nrb/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nrb">@nrb</a>)</li>
<li>Azure: support using <code>aad-pod-identity</code> auth when using restic (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="629576234" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2602" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2602/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2602">#2602</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skriss/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skriss">@skriss</a>)</li>
<li>log a warning instead of erroring if an additional item returned from a plugin can't be found in the Kubernetes API (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="628704830" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2595" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2595/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2595">#2595</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skriss/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skriss">@skriss</a>)</li>
<li>when creating new backup from schedule from cli, allow backup name to be automatically generated (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="624032649" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2569" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2569/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2569">#2569</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/cblecker/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/cblecker">@cblecker</a>)</li>
<li>Convert manifests + BSL api client to kubebuilder (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="622864315" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2561" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2561/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2561">#2561</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/carlisia/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/carlisia">@carlisia</a>)</li>
<li>backup/restore: reinstantiate backup store just before uploading artifacts to ensure credentials are up-to-date (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="621974373" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2550" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2550/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2550">#2550</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skriss/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skriss">@skriss</a>)</li>

  <div class="markdown-body">
    <h2>v1.5.0-rc.1</h2>
<h3>2020-09-09</h3>
<h3>Download</h3>
<p><a href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.5.0-rc.1">https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.5.0-rc.1</a></p>
<h3>Container Image</h3>
<p><code>velero/velero:v1.5.0-rc.1</code></p>
<h3>Documentation</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.5.0-rc.1/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.5.0-rc.1/</a></p>
<h3>Upgrading</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.5.0-rc.1/upgrade-to-1.5/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.5.0-rc.1/upgrade-to-1.5/</a></p>
<h3>Highlights</h3>
<ul>
<li>Auto Volume Backup Using Restic with <code>--default-volumes-to-restic</code> flag</li>
<li>DeleteItemAction plugins</li>
<li>Code modernization</li>
<li>Restore Hooks: InitContianer Restore Hooks and Exec Restore Hooks</li>
</ul>
<h3>All Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li>Use format version instead of version on <code>velero backup describe</code> since version has been deprecated (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="692781619" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2901" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2901/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2901">#2901</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jenting/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jenting">@jenting</a>)</li>
<li>Implement post-restore exec hooks in pod containers (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="675413295" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2804" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2804/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2804">#2804</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/areed/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/areed">@areed</a>)</li>
<li>rename the PV if VolumeSnapshotter has modified the PV name (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="681281267" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2835" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2835/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2835">#2835</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/pawanpraka1/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/pawanpraka1">@pawanpraka1</a>)</li>
<li>fix EnableAPIGroupersions output log format (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="689908486" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2882" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2882/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2882">#2882</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jenting/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jenting">@jenting</a>)</li>
<li>Convert ServerStatusRequest controller to kubebuilder (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="681388286" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2838" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2838/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2838">#2838</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/carlisia/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/carlisia">@carlisia</a>)</li>
<li>Check for errors on restic backup command (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="685092169" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2863" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2863/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2863">#2863</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/dymurray/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/dymurray">@dymurray</a>)</li>
<li><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="bug" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f41b.png">🐛</g-emoji> fix passing LDFLAGS across build stages (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="683831848" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2853" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2853/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2853">#2853</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ashish-amarnath/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ashish-amarnath">@ashish-amarnath</a>)</li>
<li>Feature: Invoke DeleteItemAction plugins based on backup contents when a backup is deleted. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="677936479" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2815" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2815/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2815">#2815</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nrb/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nrb">@nrb</a>)</li>
<li>When JSON logging format is enabled, place error message at "error.message" instead of "error" for compatibility with Elasticsearch/ELK and the Elastic Common Schema (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="680286571" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2830" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2830/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2830">#2830</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/bgagnon/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/bgagnon">@bgagnon</a>)</li>
<li>Add the DeleteItemAction plugin type (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="676470306" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2808" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2808/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2808">#2808</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nrb/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nrb">@nrb</a>)</li>
<li>discovery Helper support get GroupVersionResource and an APIResource from GroupVersionKind (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="665731515" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2764" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2764/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2764">#2764</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/runzexia/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/runzexia">@runzexia</a>)</li>
<li><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="bug" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f41b.png">🐛</g-emoji> Manually patch the generated yaml for restore CRD as a hacky workaround (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="677340474" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2814" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2814/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2814">#2814</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ashish-amarnath/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ashish-amarnath">@ashish-amarnath</a>)</li>

  <div class="markdown-body">
    <h2>v1.5.0-beta.1</h2>
<h3>2020-08-21</h3>
<h3>Download</h3>
<p><a href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.5.0-beta.1">https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.5.0-beta.1</a></p>
<h3>Container Image</h3>
<p><code>velero/velero:v1.5.0-beta.1</code></p>
<h3>Documentation</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.5-pre/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.5-pre/</a></p>
<h3>Upgrading</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.5-pre/upgrade-to-1.5/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.5-pre/upgrade-to-1.5/</a></p>
<h3>Highlights</h3>
<ul>
<li>Auto Volume Backup Using Restic with <code>--default-volumes-to-restic</code> flag</li>
<li>DeleteItemAction plugins</li>
<li>Code modernization</li>
<li>Sneak preview - restore hooks using init containers</li>
</ul>
<h3>All Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li>Feature: Invoke DeleteItemAction plugins based on backup contents when a backup is deleted. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="677936479" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2815" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2815/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2815">#2815</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nrb/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nrb">@nrb</a>)</li>
<li>When JSON logging format is enabled, place error message at "error.message" instead of "error" for compatibility with Elasticsearch/ELK and the Elastic Common Schema (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="680286571" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2830" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2830/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2830">#2830</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/bgagnon/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/bgagnon">@bgagnon</a>)</li>
<li>discovery Helper support get GroupVersionResource and an APIResource from GroupVersionKind (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="665731515" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2764" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2764/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2764">#2764</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/runzexia/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/runzexia">@runzexia</a>)</li>
<li>Migrate site from Jekyll to Hugo (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="659666877" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2720" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2720/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2720">#2720</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/tbatard/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/tbatard">@tbatard</a>)</li>
<li>Add the DeleteItemAction plugin type (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="676470306" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2808" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2808/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2808">#2808</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nrb/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nrb">@nrb</a>)</li>
<li><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="bug" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f41b.png">🐛</g-emoji> Manually patch the generated yaml for restore CRD as a hacky workaround (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="677340474" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2814" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2814/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2814">#2814</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ashish-amarnath/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ashish-amarnath">@ashish-amarnath</a>)</li>

<li>log a warning instead of erroring if an additional item returned from a plugin can't be found in the Kubernetes API (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="628704830" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2595" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2595/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2595">#2595</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skriss/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skriss">@skriss</a>)</li>
<li>when creating new backup from schedule from cli, allow backup name to be automatically generated (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="624032649" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2569" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2569/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2569">#2569</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/cblecker/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/cblecker">@cblecker</a>)</li>
<li>Convert manifests + BSL api client to kubebuilder (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="622864315" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2561" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2561/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2561">#2561</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/carlisia/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/carlisia">@carlisia</a>)</li>

  <div class="markdown-body">
    <h2>v1.4.2</h2>
<h3>2020-07-13</h3>
<h3>Download</h3>
<p><a href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.4.2">https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.4.2</a></p>
<h3>Container Image</h3>
<p><code>velero/velero:v1.4.2</code></p>
<h3>Documentation</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.4/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.4/</a></p>
<h3>Upgrading</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.4/upgrade-to-1.4/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.4/upgrade-to-1.4/</a></p>
<h3>All Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li>log a warning instead of erroring if an additional item returned from a plugin can't be found in the Kubernetes API (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="628704830" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2595" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2595/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2595">#2595</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skriss/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skriss">@skriss</a>)</li>
<li>Adjust restic default time out to 4 hours and base pod resource requests to 500m CPU/512Mi memory. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="652550053" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2696" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2696/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2696">#2696</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nrb/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nrb">@nrb</a>)</li>
<li>capture version of the CRD prior before invoking the remap_crd_version backup item action (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="650181904" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2683" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2683/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2683">#2683</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ashish-amarnath/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ashish-amarnath">@ashish-amarnath</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h2>v1.4.1</h2>
<p>This tag was created in code, but has no associated docker image due to misconfigured building infrastructure. v1.4.2 fixes this.</p>

  <div class="markdown-body">
    <h2>v1.4.0</h2>
<h3>2020-05-26</h3>
<h3>Download</h3>
<p><a href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.4.0">https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.4.0</a></p>
<h3>Container Image</h3>
<p><code>velero/velero:v1.4.0</code></p>
<h3>Documentation</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.4/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.4/</a></p>
<h3>Upgrading</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.4/upgrade-to-1.4/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.4/upgrade-to-1.4/</a></p>
<h3>Highlights</h3>
<ul>
<li>Added beta-level CSI support!</li>
<li>Added custom CA certificate support</li>
<li>Backup progress reporting</li>
<li>Changed backup tarball format to support all versions of a given resource</li>
</ul>
<h3>All Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li>increment restic volumesnapshot count after successful pvb create (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="619309665" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2542" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2542/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2542">#2542</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ashish-amarnath/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ashish-amarnath">@ashish-amarnath</a>)</li>
<li>Add details of CSI volumesnapshotcontents associated with a backup to <code>velero backup describe</code> when the <code>EnableCSI</code> feature flag is given on the velero client. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="603562843" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2448" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2448/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2448">#2448</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nrb/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nrb">@nrb</a>)</li>
<li>Allow users the option to retrieve all versions of a given resource (instead of just the preferred version) from the API server with the <code>EnableAPIGroupVersions</code> feature flag. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="589424724" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2373" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2373/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2373">#2373</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/brito-rafa/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/brito-rafa">@brito-rafa</a>)</li>
<li>Changed backup tarball format to store all versions of a given resource, updated backup tarball format to 1.1.0. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="589424724" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2373" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2373/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2373">#2373</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/brito-rafa/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/brito-rafa">@brito-rafa</a>)</li>
<li>allow feature flags to be passed from install CLI (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="612824684" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2503" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2503/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2503">#2503</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ashish-amarnath/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ashish-amarnath">@ashish-amarnath</a>)</li>
<li>sync backups' CSI API objects into the cluster as part of the backup sync controller (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="612050886" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2496" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2496/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2496">#2496</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ashish-amarnath/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ashish-amarnath">@ashish-amarnath</a>)</li>
<li>bug fix: in error location logging hook, if the item logged under the <code>error</code> key doesn't implement the <code>error</code> interface, don't return an error since this is a valid scenario (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="610397669" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2487" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2487/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2487">#2487</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skriss/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skriss">@skriss</a>)</li>
<li>bug fix: in CRD restore plugin, don't use runtime.DefaultUnstructuredConverter.FromUnstructured(...) to avoid conversion issues when float64 fields contain int values (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="610114818" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2484" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2484/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2484">#2484</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skriss/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skriss">@skriss</a>)</li>
<li>during backup deletion also delete CSI volumesnapshotcontents that were created as a part of the backup but the associated volumesnapshot object does not exist (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="609385447" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2480" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2480/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2480">#2480</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ashish-amarnath/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ashish-amarnath">@ashish-amarnath</a>)</li>
<li>If plugins don't support the <code>--features</code> flag, don't pass it to them. Also, update the standard plugin server to ignore unknown flags. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="609347531" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2479" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2479/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2479">#2479</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skriss/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skriss">@skriss</a>)</li>
<li>At backup time, if a CustomResourceDefinition appears to have been created via the v1beta1 endpoint, retrieve it from the v1beta1 endpoint instead of simply changing the APIVersion. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="609298623" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2478" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2478/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2478">#2478</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nrb/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nrb">@nrb</a>)</li>
<li>update container base images from ubuntu:bionic to ubuntu:focal (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="608637529" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2471" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2471/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2471">#2471</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skriss/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skriss">@skriss</a>)</li>

  <div class="markdown-body">
    <h2>v1.4.0-beta.1</h2>
<h3>2020-05-08</h3>
<h3>Download</h3>
<p><a href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.4.0-beta.1">https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.4.0-beta.1</a></p>
<h3>Container Image</h3>
<p><code>velero/velero:v1.4.0-beta.1</code></p>
<h3>Documentation</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.4-pre/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.4-pre/</a></p>
<h3>Upgrading</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.4-pre/upgrade-to-1.4/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.4-pre/upgrade-to-1.4/</a></p>
<h3>Download</h3>
<p><a href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.4.0-beta.1">https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/releases/tag/v1.4.0-beta.1</a></p>
<h3>Highlights</h3>
<ul>
<li>Added beta-level CSI support</li>
<li>Added custom CA certificate support</li>
<li>Backup progress reporting</li>
</ul>
<h3>All Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li>Add details of CSI volumesnapshotcontents associated with a backup to <code>velero backup describe</code> when the <code>EnableCSI</code> feature flag is given on the velero client. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="603562843" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2448" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2448/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2448">#2448</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nrb/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nrb">@nrb</a>)</li>

<h3>All Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li>Allow <code>plugins/</code> as a valid top-level directory within backup storage locations. This directory is a place for plugin authors to store arbitrary data as needed. It is recommended to create an additional subdirectory under <code>plugins/</code> specifically for your plugin, e.g. <code>plugins/my-plugin-data/</code>. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="583169870" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2350" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2350/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2350">#2350</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skriss/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skriss">@skriss</a>)</li>
<li>bug fix: don't panic in <code>velero restic repo get</code> when last maintenance time is <code>nil</code> (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="575005222" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/issues/2315" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2315/hovercard" href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2315">#2315</a>, <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skriss/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skriss">@skriss</a>)</li>

    <h3>Container Image</h3>
<p><code>velero/velero:v1.3.0</code></p>
<h3>Documentation</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.3.0/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.3.0/</a></p>
<h3>Upgrading</h3>
<p><a href="https://velero.io/docs/v1.3.0/upgrade-to-1.3/" rel="nofollow">https://velero.io/docs/v1.3.0/upgrade-to-1.3/</a></p>
<h3>Highlights</h3>
<h4>Custom Resource Definition Backup and Restore Improvements</h4>
<p>This release includes a number of related bug fixes and improvements to how Velero backs up and restores custom resource definitions (CRDs) and instances of those CRDs.</p>
<p>We found and fixed three issues around restoring CRDs that were originally created via the <code>v1beta1</code> CRD API.  The first issue affected CRDs that  had the <code>PreserveUnknownFields</code> field set to <code>true</code>.  These CRDs could not be restored into 1.16+ Kubernetes clusters, because the <code>v1</code> CRD API does not allow this field to be set to <code>true</code>. We added code to the restore process to check for this scenario, to set the <code>PreserveUnknownFields</code> field to <code>false</code>, and to instead set <code>x-kubernetes-preserve-unknown-fields</code> to <code>true</code> in the OpenAPIv3 structural schema, per Kubernetes guidance. For more information on this, see the <a href="https://kubernetes.io/docs/tasks/access-kubernetes-api/custom-resources/custom-resource-definitions/#pruning-versus-preserving-unknown-fields" rel="nofollow">Kubernetes documentation</a>. The second issue affected CRDs without structural schemas. These CRDs need to be backed up/restored through the <code>v1beta1</code> API, since all CRDs created through the <code>v1</code> API must have structural schemas. We added code to detect these CRDs and always back them up/restore them through the <code>v1beta1</code> API. Finally, related to the previous issue, we found that our restore code was unable to handle backups with multiple API versions for a given resource type, and we’ve remediated this as well.</p>
<p>We also improved the CRD restore process to enable users to properly restore CRDs and instances of those CRDs in a single restore operation. Previously, users found that they needed to run two separate restores: one to restore the CRD(s), and another to restore instances of the CRD(s).  This was due to two deficiencies in the Velero code. First, Velero did not wait for a CRD to be fully accepted by the Kubernetes API server and ready for serving before moving on; and second, Velero did not refresh its cached list of available APIs in the target cluster after restoring CRDs, so it was not aware that it could restore instances of those CRDs.</p>
<p>We fixed both of these issues by (1) adding code to wait for CRDs to be “ready” after restore before moving on, and (2) refreshing the cached list of APIs after restoring CRDs, so any instances of newly-restored CRDs could subsequently be restored.</p>
<p>With all of these fixes and improvements in place, we hope that the CRD backup and restore experience is now seamless across all supported versions of Kubernetes.</p>
<h4>Multi-Arch Docker Images</h4>
<p>Thanks to community members <a href="https://github.com/Prajyot-Parab">@Prajyot-Parab</a> and <a href="https://github.com/shaneutt">@shaneutt</a>, Velero now provides multi-arch container images by using Docker manifest lists.  We are currently publishing images for <code>linux/amd64</code>, <code>linux/arm64</code>, <code>linux/arm</code>, and <code>linux/ppc64le</code> in <a href="https://hub.docker.com/r/velero/velero/tags?page=1&amp;name=v1.3&amp;ordering=last_updated" rel="nofollow">our Docker repository</a>.</p>
<p>Users don’t need to change anything other than updating their version tag - the v1.3 image is <code>velero/velero:v1.3.0</code>, and Docker will automatically pull the proper architecture for the host.</p>
<p>For more information on manifest lists, see <a href="https://docs.docker.com/registry/spec/manifest-v2-2/" rel="nofollow">Docker’s documentation</a>.</p>
<h4>Bug Fixes, Usability Enhancements, and More</h4>
<p>We fixed a large number of bugs and made some smaller usability improvements in this release. Here are a few highlights:</p>
<ul>
<li>Support private registries with custom ports for the restic restore helper image (<a href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/1999" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/1999/hovercard">PR #1999</a>, <a href="https://github.com/cognoz">@cognoz</a>)</li>
<li>Use AWS profile from BackupStorageLocation when invoking restic (<a href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2096" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2096/hovercard">PR #2096</a>, <a href="https://github.com/dinesh">@dinesh</a>)</li>
<li>Allow restores from schedules in other clusters (<a href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2218" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2218/hovercard">PR #2218</a>, <a href="https://github.com/cpanato">@cpanato</a>)</li>
<li>Fix memory leak &amp; race condition in restore code (<a href="https://github.com/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2201" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/vmware-tanzu/velero/pull/2201/hovercard">PR #2201</a>, <a href="https://github.com/skriss">@skriss</a>)</li>
</ul>
